help struct
 <strong>struct</strong> Create or convert to structure array.
    S = <strong>struct</strong>('field1',VALUES1,'field2',VALUES2,...) creates a
    structure array with the specified fields and values.  The value
    arrays VALUES1, VALUES2, etc. must be cell arrays of the same
    size, scalar cells or single values.  Corresponding elements of the
    value arrays are placed into corresponding structure array elements.
    The size of the resulting structure is the same size as the value
    cell arrays or 1-by-1 if none of the values is a cell.
 
    <strong>struct</strong>(OBJ) converts the object OBJ into its equivalent
    structure.  The class information is lost.
 
    <strong>struct</strong>([]) creates an empty 0-by-0 structure with no fields.
 
    To create fields that contain cell arrays, place the cell arrays
    within a VALUE cell array.  For instance,
      s = struct('strings',{{'hello','yes'}},'lengths',[5 3])
    creates the 1-by-1 structure
       s = 
          strings: {'hello'  'yes'}
          lengths: [5 3]
 
    Example
       s = struct('type',{'big','little'},'color','red','x',{3 4})
 
    See also <a href="matlab:help isstruct -displayBanner">isstruct</a>, <a href="matlab:help setfield -displayBanner">setfield</a>, <a href="matlab:help getfield -displayBanner">getfield</a>, <a href="matlab:help fieldnames -displayBanner">fieldnames</a>, <a href="matlab:help orderfields -displayBanner">orderfields</a>, 
    <a href="matlab:help isfield -displayBanner">isfield</a>, <a href="matlab:help rmfield -displayBanner">rmfield</a>, <a href="matlab:help deal -displayBanner">deal</a>, <a href="matlab:help substruct -displayBanner">substruct</a>, <a href="matlab:help struct2cell -displayBanner">struct2cell</a>, <a href="matlab:help cell2struct -displayBanner">cell2struct</a>.

    <a href="matlab:doc struct">Documentation for struct</a>
    <a href="matlab:matlab.internal.language.introspective.overloads.displayOverloads('struct')">Other uses of struct</a>
    <a href="matlab:matlab.internal.help.displayFoldersList('struct')">Folders named struct</a>
